      • addBonusPremium

        public void addBonusPremium(java.lang.CharSequence param)
        Appends the specified BonusPremium to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the code relevant for crediting premium amount to the Deposit account. It is more relevant in the case of Deposit accounts like Savings Plan/ Recurring Deposit etc., where for prompt payment of installments a certain amount will be credited to the account as bonus. Bonus is not applicable to multi deposits Validation Rules Should be a valid code defined in FT.CHARGE.TYPE, FT.COMMISSION.TYPE By prefixing ' * ' with the ID of SAVINGS.PREMIUM, it can be linked to SAVINGS.PREMIUm

        Parameters:
        param - the BonusPremium to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addChargeDrTxn

        public void addChargeDrTxn(java.lang.CharSequence param)
        Appends the specified ChargeDrTxn to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to identify the entries that are raised while charging the late payment fee. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y".

        Parameters:
        param - the ChargeDrTxn to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addDepositCr

        public void addDepositCr(java.lang.CharSequence param)
        Appends the specified DepositCr to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to signify that the entry is a deposit credit entry. If MULTI is set as 'Y' then a sub account is created else a principle increase is made. In case of clearing credits the transction code for collection, the txn code defined in CQ.PARAMETER / ACCOUNT.PARAMETER that is used when the cheque is marked as CLEARED, has to be defined here. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y".

        Parameters:
        param - the DepositCr to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addIntCorrTxn

        public void addIntCorrTxn(TField param)
        Appends the specified IntCorrTxn to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan/deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to signify that the entry is a interest correction entry. Interest correction can be for various reason like preclosure or part withdrawal in deposits etc... VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Both debit / credit transaction code allowed. Refer to INT.CR.CAP for transaction codes that need to be setup.

        Parameters:
        param - the IntCorrTxn to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addIntCrCap

        public void addIntCrCap(TField param)
        Appends the specified IntCrCap to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This pertains to AZ deposits where on Capitalisation date interest is capitalized to the credit of the deposit acct using this TXN code. Valid Transaction code should be entered. This txn code is used capitalization of interest to the deposit acct, where Credit will be to the deposit acct and debit to the interest payable category. When TXN code is entered the system will automatically identify the transaction code as event of Interest Credit Cap. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid 'ID' in Transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to 'Y' Refer to INT.DR.CAP on the specific transaction codes that need to defined..This is not applicable for ANNUITY/ CREDIT CARDS.

        Parameters:
        param - the IntCrCap to append
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan / deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Interest Dr. Cap implies the Capitalization of interest to the loan a/c- where Debit will be to the loan a/c and Credit to the Interest Receivable category. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Interest Dr. Cap. When the interest is capitalized, this CODE is used on the Debit side of the Transaction for identifying the event. In case of a loan during I schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az.account with 392/391 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.CR.CAP. In case of a deposit during I schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az.account with 382/381 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.DR.CAP. When interest is to be paid manually then these fields could be multivalued and different txn codes can be defined if needed. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in Transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCOUNT. SYNC is set to 'Y' The following table gives the txn codes that have to be defined in addition to any other txn codes. Field Name Interest liq acct Loan Deposit INT.CR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.DR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.CORR.TXN Yes 396 386 No 395 385

        Parameters:
        param - the IntDrCap to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addTaxOnIntTxn

        public void addTaxOnIntTxn(TField param)
        Appends the specified TaxOnIntTxn to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan/deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to signify that the entry is a tax on interest entry when the TAX.KEY is defined in AZ.ACCOUNT. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Both debit / credit transaction code allowed. Debit/Credit transaction code should be the same as the transaction code defined in TAX table. For instance, if TAX.KEY is defined as 10 in AZ.ACCOUNT, in the respective Tax table, the Credit/debit transaction code is defined as 243/244, then the same codes should be defined here.

        Parameters:
        param - the TaxOnIntTxn to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • getAcctSync

        public TField getAcctSync()
        Returns the AcctSync

        Field description: Allowed values are 'YES' and ''. If 'YES' then the working balance in a/c and the principal in AZ.ACCOUNT created will be in sync. This can be achieved by using specific transaction codes for specific AZ related events. (For more details on transaction codes and events, refer the help text for various fields like DRAWDOWN.TXN). If the input is 'NULL', the two balances might not be in harmony. If 'YES', then an entry over the AZ.ACCOUNT should contain a valid txn code (apart from DR.TXN.CODE and CR.TXN.CODE) defined in its APP so that it knows how to process the entry within AZ. VALIDATIONS Permitted values either 'YES' or ''. Once input the values cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AcctSync

      • getAllowedCateg

        public TField getAllowedCateg()
        Returns the AllowedCateg

        Field description: The default category to which the All in One product is allocated. It is ensured by the system that all AZ accounts opened under this product, belong to the category entered here. The category code is used to classify financial transactions in T24 according to the type of business operations or product type. The first two digits represents the highest level classification and next three digits represents sub classification which provides a clear definition of the profit and loss or the product type. The use of these codes with personal customer characteristics (like Residence, Status, Sector code etc.,) will enable the Banks to produce balance sheets and returns reflecting a coordinated and structured view of its operation, by directing business transactions to their appropriate place in the report. Validation Rules 5-7 Numeric Codes It must be an existing code in the CATEGORY table For customer Accounts, it must be in the range of 1000 to 9999 The category is defaulted to AZ.ACCOUNT from the corresponding ACCOUNT record and validated against the category code defined here.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AllowedCateg

      • getApplyPenalty

        public TField getApplyPenalty()
        Returns the ApplyPenalty

        Field description: Identifies whether or not penalty is to be applied to accounts of this product. If 'Y' is defined, for loan products, penal interest will be applied on arrears automatically by the system. If 'N' is defined penalty will not be applied automatically. The user has to apply manually, if required. This field is not applicable for DEPOSIT type, as the rate of interest for redemption will be automatically calculated by the system based on the value provided in other fields like, PI.TABLE.TO.USE, PI.METHOD. Validation Rules Valid options are 'Y', 'N'. Default is 'N'.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The ApplyPenalty

      • getAppropriateType

        public TField getAppropriateType()
        Returns the AppropriateType

        Field description: This field decides how a repayment received should be apportioned among the various withdrawals made under a Credit Card account. Permitted inputs are (1) Proportionate and (2) FIFO [First in First Out]. TO ILLUSTRATE: - Suppose there are 3 draws through sub a/c Withdrawal 1 350000 Withdrawal 2 650000 Withdrawal 3 250000 TOTAL 1250000 Appropriation Type- Proportionate If the repayment received, is 125000 the set-off will be 125000*350000/1250000 Towards Drawl (1) -35000 ----I.e.- 125000*350000/1250000 Towards Drawl, (2) it is 65000--I.e.- 125000*650000/1250000 Finally toward drawl (3) 25000--I.e.- 125000*250000/1250000 Appropriation Type- FIFO If on the other hand the repayment received is, say 450000 and type is FIFO then: - First withdrawal of 350000 will be fully adjusted and then remaining amount of 100000 will be adjusted towards the O/s of second withdrawal. This way it will continue until the last drawl is met with fully. VALIDATIONS: Input can be either Proportionate or FIFO. Input is subject to change. Allowed only for CREDIT CARD type of products.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AppropriateType

      • getCcPrGracePeriod

        public TField getCcPrGracePeriod()
        Returns the CcPrGracePeriod

        Field description: For any repayment type if the GENERATION of CC schedules (principal repayment schedule) is to be postponed then this field is used. Input permitted in this field is Numeric and it should be read along with the frequency input in the repay date field of card issue application. When a card issue frequency is monthly and input made in this field is 3, it means for 3 months the generation of CC schedule is to be postponed, i.e., NO CC schedule is generated. If in card issue the frequency is weekly then it is to be interpreted that 'CC' schedules will not be generated for 3 weeks. For a Non Redemption type, input in this field is mandatory. This is for the reason that in Non Redemption type CI (interest) schedules are generated regularly and the Principal (CC schedules) repayment is made in one BULLET payment. VALIDATIONS Input allowed only if the Repayment Type is a Non redemption Allowed only for CREDIT CARD type of products.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CcPrGracePeriod

      • getCrIntFqu

        public TField getCrIntFqu()
        Returns the CrIntFqu

        Field description: Defines the frequency for interest credit, for all deposit accounts opened under this product. Example If 'M01' is defined here, this frequency will be defaulted to the deposit account of this product and interest will be credited / capitalised every month from the start date. This is acheived by defaulting the 'I' schedule into the az.account during creation. If a liquidation account is defined in ACCOUNT then interest will be credited to that account as per this frequency. Otherwise the interest will be capitalised in the Deposit account itself If 'NM01' is defined here, then the interest will be paid out to the nominated account after capitalising it every month from the start date. This is acheived by defaulting the 'IN' schedule into the az.account during creation. This field is also used during deposit rollover. Based on the setup done here either a 'I' or 'IN' schedule will be created during rollover. If this is not defined then the 'IN' schedule will be created on maturity after rollover. Validation Rules Type of input allowed are: Dnn,Wnn, Mnn

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CrIntFqu

      • getDrawdownType

        public TField getDrawdownType()
        Returns the DrawdownType

        Field description: Defines a type of drawdown for this product, which specifies the method of withdrawing the Principal amount, from the loan accounts of this product. The various types of drawdowns are: 1. Full Drawdown: The entire loan amount has to be withdrawn at a time. No partial withdrawals are allowed 2. Partial and No interest: Partial or full withdrawal of the loan amount is permitted from the loan account. Interest and Principal repayment need not be done during the drawdown period. 3. Partial and interest: The drawdown of loan amount can be done in partial or in full. During the drawdown period repayment towards interest has to be made. Otherwise it will be treated as arrears. If a nominated account is defined, in all the options, the system will automatically transfer the drawdown amount on the drawdown date to the nominated account. If no nominated account is defined and if the drawdown is preferred through the AZ account itself, then a teller default will be created and the amount can be drawn through teller using the teller default feature. Validation Rules Valid for Loan products only. Valid numbers are 1,2,3. Default is 1 (Full Drawdown) Must be 1 for CREDIT CARD type of loans.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The DrawdownType

VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Both debit / credit transaction code allowed. Refer to INT.CR.CAP for transaction codes that need to be setup.

      • getIntDrCap

        public TField getIntDrCap(int idx)
        Returns the IntDrCap at the specified position in this collection.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan / deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Interest Dr. Cap implies the Capitalization of interest to the loan a/c- where Debit will be to the loan a/c and Credit to the Interest Receivable category. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Interest Dr. Cap. When the interest is capitalized, this CODE is used on the Debit side of the Transaction for identifying the event. In case of a loan during I schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az.account with 392/391 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.CR.CAP. In case of a deposit during I schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az.account with 382/381 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.DR.CAP. When interest is to be paid manually then these fields could be multivalued and different txn codes can be defined if needed. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in Transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCOUNT. SYNC is set to 'Y' The following table gives the txn codes that have to be defined in addition to any other txn codes. Field Name Interest liq acct Loan Deposit INT.CR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.DR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.CORR.TXN Yes 396 386 No 395 385

        Parameters:
        idx - idx of the element to return
        Returns:
        TField -

      • getLastDayIncl

        public TField getLastDayIncl()
        Returns the LastDayIncl

        Field description: This field determines whether the cap date is considered for interest calculation or not. Valid inputs are 'Y' or NULL. 1. If 'Y', the interest calculation, will consider the balance as of the Cap date and post the entries with the value date of cap date + 1. 2. If null, in the interest calculation, the interest will be calculated for the balance of cap date -1, and the entries will be posted with the value date of processing date. In case of online loan repayment resulting in interest capitalisation/collection , LAST.DAY.INCL is considered to be 'N' even if LAST.DAY.INCL is 'Y' in AZ/APP Level. Validation This field is a noinput field for ANNUITY type of repayment.

      • getMaxInstlIntOnly

        public TField getMaxInstlIntOnly()
        Returns the MaxInstlIntOnly

        Field description: Total period of time that the interest only repayment could be defined for a loan during the life time of a loan account. If input is given in numbers it is treated as number of days. If input is given prefixing P, it is treated as number of installments. Example: If input is given as 60, it implies that the total number of Interest Only repayment period cannot exceed 60 days during the life of the loan account. If input is given as P60, it implies that the total number Interest only repayment period cannot exceed 60 installments (of any frequency like daily, monthly) during the life of the loan account. Note: For loan accounts with repayment type 'Non Redemption', no validation will be done with respect to this field. Validation Rules Value for this field will be accepted only if 'INT ONLY' field is defined as Y Valid only for Loan Product Cannot have negative values

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The MaxInstlIntOnly

      • getRatePeriod

        public TField getRatePeriod()
        Returns the RatePeriod

        Field description: Input in this field implies that the product is a Fixed Floating type. A Fixed Floating product initially takes a FIXED rate of interest and then moves to floating rate of interest till maturity based on the PERIOD input in the field RATE.PERIOD. Values may be input in the following format, i.e. nnD or nnM or nny The floating rate is prompted by 'R' schedule without which a FIXED FLOATING deposit or loan acct cannot be committed or authorized. The rates of interest both FIXED and FLOATING are defaulted from APP. A combination of the following interest is permitted for input, (1) BASIC.INTEREST (BI) and FIXED.RATE (2) BASIC.INTEREST (BI) and PERIODIC INTEREST (PI) To illustrate, In AZ.PRODUCT.PARAMETER the RATE.PERIOD is input as 03M. The Fixed Floating Deposit Start date is 05.04.2003 and maturity date is 04.04.2004. Interest is FIXED at 20% (field INT.FIXED.RATE) and for floating BI rate with RATE.KEY as 01 RATE.SPREAD as 2% RATE.OPERAND as ADD [Assume that the BI rate on the date of R schedule is 6.75%] System takes FIXED rate of interest at 20% from 05.04.2003 to 05.07.2003 And FLOATING rate at 8.75% (6.75% + 2%) from 06.07.2003 till 04.04.2004 Thus RATE.PERIOD is the field that differentiates a FIXED-FLOATING contract from other types of contracts. Based on the input in this field 'R' schedule is triggered to bring FLOATING rate in to operation. VALIDATIONS (1) Two numeric and One alphanumeric input allowed. (2) Permitted values in RATE.PERIOD nn>D, nn>M and nn>Y (3) Fixed and Floating interest rates are defaulted from APP- user has the option to change the FIXED rate of interest directly at account level and FLOATING rate by changing the INTEREST. RATE value in BI table. (4) The change in Rate. key value can be gauged from the ACI record only (5) Spread cannot be changed it is fixed. (6) For fixed floating a combination of BI + PI, BI + FIXED is allowed but not PI AND FIXED. (7) Not applicable for credit cards

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The RatePeriod

      • getReduceLimit

        public TField getReduceLimit()
        Returns the ReduceLimit

        Field description: This field is used to provide a revolving limit functionlity in loan products. If defined as '' then on the scheduled dates the limit is reduced for P and A schedules and incase of N schedules where there is no interest liquadation account, which provides a non-revolving functionlity. If defined as 'NO' then on the scheduled dates the limit is not reduced which provides a revolving limit functionlity. In this case the PRINCIPAL in AZ.ACCOUNT is not reduced on schedule dates or when the principal is repaid. Not allowed for deposits and CREDIT CARD. 'NO' not allowed for ANNUITY type of loans.       • getRepaymentType

        public TField getRepaymentType()
        Returns the RepaymentType

        Field description: Defines the Repayment type of the All in One Accounts opened under this product. This type determines the way in which the loan / deposit account is to be repaid. The repayment types available for loan accounts are: 1. ANNUITY This type of loan has a fixed periodic repayment amount (the 'annuity') consisting of two variable components of principal and interest. The repayment amount is calculated at the start of the contract so that the principal will be fully repaid after the required number of repayments. Initially, repayments consist mostly of interest. However, as the contract progresses, the size of the principal component increases as the accrued interest reduces. In All in One loan account, for defining a zero repayment at the start of the loan, for a fixed period, Annuity type of repayment can be defined in the schedule with amount as Zero. 2. LINEAR Linear loans also have an interest and a principal component to their periodic repayments. In this case, however, the principal repayment amount remains fixed over the lifetime of the contract. The interest element reduces as the accrued interest on the reducing balance decreases. This leads to a repayment scheme whereby the total periodic repayment reduces over the lifetime of the contract. 3. NONRED In NONRED type of loans, there is no regular repayment of principal, but only interest. The redemption of Principal will be done on maturity date of the loan. In All in One account loans, the validations relating to Interest Only and Maximum Period interest only will not happen for this type of loan. 4. OTHER Non structured repayments are handled under this type. Repayment of any amount on any dates are allowed, provided the total repayment amount is equal to principal. 5.CREDIT CARD This type of Loan repayment type was added from G14.0.00. For this repayment type, the schedules are NO. When the repayment type is Credit Card the regular schedules are discarded, sub a/cs are created and new types of schedules like CI, CC are generated automatically. Repayment types available for Deposit accounts are: FIXED Deposit amount is accepted in a fixed lump sum and repaid as fixed amount either with interest accumulated or not. SAVING PLAN Deposit amount is accepted in a periodic basis and the principal is increased in a recurring manner till the end of a fixed term. Validation Rules 1 to 12 Alpha characters. Input must be either 'ANNUITY', 'LINEAR', 'OTHERS', 'NONRED' or 'CREDIT CARD' for loan products and 'SAVINGS PLAN' or 'FIXED' for Deposit products. Once defined and record authorised cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The RepaymentType

      • getRollMatWrkDay

        public TField getRollMatWrkDay()
        Returns the RollMatWrkDay

        Field description: This field indicates if the rolled over new maturity date should be a working day or not. If the field is Yes, during rollover of loans & deposits, if the new maturity date happens to be on a holiday, then the system shall set the new maturity date to the first working day after the rolled over date. Assume that value date of AZ is 10th Aug 2005 & maturity date is 15th Aug 2005 . Then during rollover, the system shall set Value date as 15th Aug & new maturity date as 20th Aug. If the field is YES & 20th Aug happens to be a holiday & first working day after rollover is 22nd Aug , then new maturity date will be set to 22nd Aug. If the field is NO, then new maturity date will still be 20th Aug only. Allowed values - YES,NO. NO & null are treated the same.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The RollMatWrkDay

      • getRolloverAcctng

        public TField getRolloverAcctng()
        Returns the RolloverAcctng

        Field description: This field specifies if accounting entries over the AZ.ACCOUNT need to be raised during rollover. This could be useful for passbook printing purposes. For example, Let us assume that the deposit is for 5000. If the MATURITY.INSTR is 'AUTOMATIC ROLLOVER' then during rollover the following entries will be generated. A. Nominated account is given, Case 1. Rollover amount - 5000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Nominated a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Dr Nominated a/c 5000 Case 2. Rollover amount - 6000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Nominated a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 6000 Dr Nominated a/c 6000 Case 3. Rollover amount - 4000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Nominated a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 4000 Dr Nominated a/c 4000 B. No nominated account given, Case 1. Rollover amount - 5000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Internal a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Dr Internal a/c 5000 Case 2. Rollover amount - 6000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Internal a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 6000 Dr Internal a/c 6000 Create a TELLER.DEFAULT crediting AZ.ACCOUNT for 1000. Case 3. Rollover amount - 4000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Internal a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 4000 Dr Internal a/c 4000 Create a TELLER.DEFAULT debiting Internal account for 1000. MATURITY.DR txn code will be used on the debit side and ROLLOVER.CR txn code will be used on the credit side entries to AZ.ACCOUNT. If nominated account is not provided then an internal account will be used. The category of the internal account need to be defined in ACCOUNT.CLASS application for 'AZROLLOVER' id. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Debit transction code defined in the TAX file.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        List<TField> -

      • getTaxOnIntTxn

        public List<TField> getTaxOnIntTxn()
        Returns the collection of TaxOnIntTxn

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan/deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to signify that the entry is a tax on interest entry when the TAX.KEY is defined in AZ.ACCOUNT. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Both debit / credit transaction code allowed. Debit/Credit transaction code should be the same as the transaction code defined in TAX table. For instance, if TAX.KEY is defined as 10 in AZ.ACCOUNT, in the respective Tax table, the Credit/debit transaction code is defined as 243/244, then the same codes should be defined here.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        List<TField> -

      • getTermPriority

        public TField getTermPriority()
        Returns the TermPriority

        Field description: Specifies whether the Term of the loan has to be prioritised and kept constant or not, in the case of Re scheduling. In AZ Loan accounts, the term of the loan or repayment amount may change due to certain factors like Principal increase, Principal decrease, change in Rate of interest, change in frequency etc. In such cases, it is possible to retain the original term and the maturity date as constant and change the repayment amount suitably, by specifying the Term Priority as 'Y'. If Term Priority is specified as 'N', then by keeping the repayment amount as constant the term will be changed by altering the maturity date of the loan. This field has to be opted by the user whenever a Rescheduling of the loan account is to be done. According to the value defined here, Rescheduling will be done and the previous schedule will be written to AZ.SCHEDULES.HIST. In case of annuity type of loans if the user defined annuity amount is greater than the system generated amount then the contract will be matured earlier than the actual maturity date even though this field is set to 'Y'. In case of OTHERS/NONRED type of loans, TERM.PRIORITY 'N' is not applicable as they may have uneven payments. Hence if AZ contract is of OTHERS/NONRED type of loans, then system shall ignore the value in this field and work as if TERM.PRIORITY is 'Y'. Validation Rules Valid value 'Y' or 'N'

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The TermPriority

      • insertIntDrCap

        public void insertIntDrCap(TField param, int pos)
        Insert the specified IntDrCap to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan / deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Interest Dr. Cap implies the Capitalization of interest to the loan a/c- where Debit will be to the loan a/c and Credit to the Interest Receivable category. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Interest Dr. Cap. When the interest is capitalized, this CODE is used on the Debit side of the Transaction for identifying the event. In case of a loan during I schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az.account with 392/391 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.CR.CAP. In case of a deposit during I schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az.account with 382/381 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.DR.CAP. When interest is to be paid manually then these fields could be multivalued and different txn codes can be defined if needed. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in Transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCOUNT. SYNC is set to 'Y' The following table gives the txn codes that have to be defined in addition to any other txn codes. Field Name Interest liq acct Loan Deposit INT.CR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.DR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.CORR.TXN Yes 396 386 No 395 385

        Parameters:
        param - the IntDrCap to append
        pos - The position where to insert the value.
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan/deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to signify that the entry is a tax on interest entry when the TAX.KEY is defined in AZ.ACCOUNT. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Both debit / credit transaction code allowed. Debit/Credit transaction code should be the same as the transaction code defined in TAX table. For instance, if TAX.KEY is defined as 10 in AZ.ACCOUNT, in the respective Tax table, the Credit/debit transaction code is defined as 243/244, then the same codes should be defined here.

        Parameters:
        param - the TaxOnIntTxn to append
        pos - The position where to insert the value.
        Returns:
        nothing

      • removeIntDrCap

        public void removeIntDrCap(int idx)
        Remove the IntDrCap at the specified position in this collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan / deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Interest Dr. Cap implies the Capitalization of interest to the loan a/c- where Debit will be to the loan a/c and Credit to the Interest Receivable category. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Interest Dr. Cap. When the interest is capitalized, this CODE is used on the Debit side of the Transaction for identifying the event. In case of a loan during I schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az.account with 392/391 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.CR.CAP. In case of a deposit during I schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az.account with 382/381 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.DR.CAP. When interest is to be paid manually then these fields could be multivalued and different txn codes can be defined if needed. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in Transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCOUNT. SYNC is set to 'Y' The following table gives the txn codes that have to be defined in addition to any other txn codes. Field Name Interest liq acct Loan Deposit INT.CR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.DR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.CORR.TXN Yes 396 386 No 395 385

        Parameters:
        idx - index of the element to remove
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setAcctSync

        public void setAcctSync(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for AcctSync
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Allowed values are 'YES' and ''. If 'YES' then the working balance in a/c and the principal in AZ.ACCOUNT created will be in sync. This can be achieved by using specific transaction codes for specific AZ related events. (For more details on transaction codes and events, refer the help text for various fields like DRAWDOWN.TXN). If the input is 'NULL', the two balances might not be in harmony. If 'YES', then an entry over the AZ.ACCOUNT should contain a valid txn code (apart from DR.TXN.CODE and CR.TXN.CODE) defined in its APP so that it knows how to process the entry within AZ. VALIDATIONS Permitted values either 'YES' or ''. Once input the values cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setAllowedCateg

        public void setAllowedCateg(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for AllowedCateg
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The default category to which the All in One product is allocated. It is ensured by the system that all AZ accounts opened under this product, belong to the category entered here. The category code is used to classify financial transactions in T24 according to the type of business operations or product type. The first two digits represents the highest level classification and next three digits represents sub classification which provides a clear definition of the profit and loss or the product type. The use of these codes with personal customer characteristics (like Residence, Status, Sector code etc.,) will enable the Banks to produce balance sheets and returns reflecting a coordinated and structured view of its operation, by directing business transactions to their appropriate place in the report. Validation Rules 5-7 Numeric Codes It must be an existing code in the CATEGORY table For customer Accounts, it must be in the range of 1000 to 9999 The category is defaulted to AZ.ACCOUNT from the corresponding ACCOUNT record and validated against the category code defined here.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setAppropriateType

        public void setAppropriateType(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AppropriateType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field decides how a repayment received should be apportioned among the various withdrawals made under a Credit Card account. Permitted inputs are (1) Proportionate and (2) FIFO [First in First Out]. TO ILLUSTRATE: - Suppose there are 3 draws through sub a/c Withdrawal 1 350000 Withdrawal 2 650000 Withdrawal 3 250000 TOTAL 1250000 Appropriation Type- Proportionate If the repayment received, is 125000 the set-off will be 125000*350000/1250000 Towards Drawl (1) -35000 ----I.e.- 125000*350000/1250000 Towards Drawl, (2) it is 65000--I.e.- 125000*650000/1250000 Finally toward drawl (3) 25000--I.e.- 125000*250000/1250000 Appropriation Type- FIFO If on the other hand the repayment received is, say 450000 and type is FIFO then: - First withdrawal of 350000 will be fully adjusted and then remaining amount of 100000 will be adjusted towards the O/s of second withdrawal. This way it will continue until the last drawl is met with fully. VALIDATIONS: Input can be either Proportionate or FIFO. Input is subject to change. Allowed only for CREDIT CARD type of products.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        public void setBonusOn(java.lang.CharSequence value)

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: "This field defines the base amount on which bonus is to be calculated for deposits of SAVINGS PLAN type. If defined as 'PRINCIPAL' then the bonus will be calcuated on the amount in the PRINCIPAL field in AZ.ACCOUNT. If defined as 'INTEREST' then the bonus will be calculated on the interest that has been capitalised so far. If '' then the bonus will be calculated on the WORKING.BALANCE of the account. If MULTI is set to 'YES' then the base amount will be the sum of the amounts of the valid sub accounts. Allowed values are 'PRINCIPAL', 'INTEREST' and ''. This field should be read along with BONUS.ON.ARREARS.

      • setCcPrGracePeriod

        public void setCcPrGracePeriod(TField value)
        Set the specified value for CcPrGracePeriod
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: For any repayment type if the GENERATION of CC schedules (principal repayment schedule) is to be postponed then this field is used. Input permitted in this field is Numeric and it should be read along with the frequency input in the repay date field of card issue application. When a card issue frequency is monthly and input made in this field is 3, it means for 3 months the generation of CC schedule is to be postponed, i.e., NO CC schedule is generated. If in card issue the frequency is weekly then it is to be interpreted that 'CC' schedules will not be generated for 3 weeks. For a Non Redemption type, input in this field is mandatory. This is for the reason that in Non Redemption type CI (interest) schedules are generated regularly and the Principal (CC schedules) repayment is made in one BULLET payment. VALIDATIONS Input allowed only if the Repayment Type is a Non redemption Allowed only for CREDIT CARD type of products.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCrDepFqu

        public void setCrDepFqu(TField value)
        Set the specified value for CrDepFqu
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the frequency of further credits to the deposit account. In the case of deposits like Savings Plan, Recurring Deposit, this field is use for defining the frequency of future credits expected. For example, if M01 is defined here, regular monthly credits to the account are expected. Validation Rules Type of input allowed are: D<nn>,W<nn>, M<nn>. This field and grace period field should have a rationale input i.e. Grace can't be Month. End while the deposit frequency is daily. This validation is valid from 14.2.00 with the introduction of period. end option in Grace period field.

        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCrIntFqu

        public void setCrIntFqu(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for CrIntFqu
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the frequency for interest credit, for all deposit accounts opened under this product. Example If 'M01' is defined here, this frequency will be defaulted to the deposit account of this product and interest will be credited / capitalised every month from the start date. This is acheived by defaulting the 'I' schedule into the az.account during creation. If a liquidation account is defined in ACCOUNT then interest will be credited to that account as per this frequency. Otherwise the interest will be capitalised in the Deposit account itself If 'NM01' is defined here, then the interest will be paid out to the nominated account after capitalising it every month from the start date. This is acheived by defaulting the 'IN' schedule into the az.account during creation. This field is also used during deposit rollover. Based on the setup done here either a 'I' or 'IN' schedule will be created during rollover. If this is not defined then the 'IN' schedule will be created on maturity after rollover. Validation Rules Type of input allowed are: Dnn,Wnn, Mnn

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCrTxnCode

        public void setCrTxnCode(TField value)
        Set the specified value for CrTxnCode
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Transaction Code to be used on the Credit entry generated by AZ. The Transaction Code of the entry is used to determine the references and narratives to be printed on statements. The Debit/Credit indicators within the Transaction Code table are not used to verify this input. If the ACCT.SYNC field is "Y" -then the transaction code defined here might be used as a default for the other leg of the transaction that it not affecting the loan. The transaction code defined here should be used or duplicated in any other field. See example in DR.TXN.CODE. Validation Rules 1-3 numeric character Transaction code. (Mandatory input.) Must be an existing code in Transaction Table.

        value - The value to set

      • setCreatePdEod

        public void setCreatePdEod(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for CreatePdEod
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: For CREDIT CARD type of products this field indicates if PD has to be created during COB on the schedule dates if the repay account has insufficient funds. If set as 'YES' then PD will be created during COB, else PD will have to created through a online payment beyond the schedule date. This field is valid only for CREDIT CARD type of products. This field is allowed only if PD.LINK.TO.AZ.is set to 'YES'. Allowed values are 'YES', 'NO', ''. 'NO' and '' are considered to be the same. For credit cards, system has to settles first by date wise and then by component wise. Hence related PD.PARAMETER should have REPAYMENT.METHOD as '3' and only the following components are settled by AZ and in the order REPAYMENT.ORDER as A1,TX,A2,PE,PS,IN,Pr

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field indicates whether to create TELLER.DEFAULT or not for the interest amount during part withdrawal(through TELLER) /Pre closure when till account is used as credit side account. . This will only be created when no nominated/interest liquidation is specified on the AZ.ACCOUNT. If the field CREATE.TD.FOR.INT is NULL the interest will be credited to the credit side account irrespective of it being the till account.         public void setDrTxnCode(TField value)
        Set the specified value for DrTxnCode
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Transaction Code to be used on the Debit entry generated by AZ. The Transaction Code of the entry is used to determine the references and narratives to be printed on statements. The Debit/Credit indicators within the Transaction Code table are not used to verify this input. The transaction code defined here should be used or duplicated in any other field. If the ACCT.SYNC field is "Y" -then the transaction code defined here might be used as a default for the other leg of the transaction that it not affecting the loan / deposit when the transaction is triggered from AZ.ACCOUNT. To exemplify, In Credit Card type of loan, if the loan repayment takes place. Dr. will be to the internal/customer/nominated a/c and credit to the loan a/c. As debit side of the transaction is not affecting the loan (debit to a customer a/c)- the transaction code will be one inscribed in this field. Validation Rules 1-3 numeric character Transaction code. (Mandatory input.) Must be an existing code in Transaction Table.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Draw down Txn implies making a draw down on the loan a/c- where Debit will be to the Loan a/c and Credit will be to the Nominated a/c. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Draw down. Whenever, loan is drawn this TXN code is used to identify the event, if ACCT.SYNC.is set to 'Y'. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid id in transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y".

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setDrawdownType

        public void setDrawdownType(TField value)
        Set the specified value for DrawdownType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines a type of drawdown for this product, which specifies the method of withdrawing the Principal amount, from the loan accounts of this product. The various types of drawdowns are: 1. Full Drawdown: The entire loan amount has to be withdrawn at a time. No partial withdrawals are allowed 2. Partial and No interest: Partial or full withdrawal of the loan amount is permitted from the loan account. Interest and Principal repayment need not be done during the drawdown period. 3. Partial and interest: The drawdown of loan amount can be done in partial or in full. During the drawdown period repayment towards interest has to be made. Otherwise it will be treated as arrears. If a nominated account is defined, in all the options, the system will automatically transfer the drawdown amount on the drawdown date to the nominated account. If no nominated account is defined and if the drawdown is preferred through the AZ account itself, then a teller default will be created and the amount can be drawn through teller using the teller default feature. Validation Rules Valid for Loan products only. Valid numbers are 1,2,3. Default is 1 (Full Drawdown) Must be 1 for CREDIT CARD type of loans.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setIntDrCap

        public void setIntDrCap(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)
        Set the specified IntDrCap to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan / deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Interest Dr. Cap implies the Capitalization of interest to the loan a/c- where Debit will be to the loan a/c and Credit to the Interest Receivable category. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Interest Dr. Cap. When the interest is capitalized, this CODE is used on the Debit side of the Transaction for identifying the event. In case of a loan during I schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az.account with 392/391 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.CR.CAP. In case of a deposit during I schedule the system would raise an entry to credit the az.account with 382/381 as the txn code. During N schedule the system would raise an entry to debit the az account with the value defined in the first multi value of INT.DR.CAP. When interest is to be paid manually then these fields could be multivalued and different txn codes can be defined if needed. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in Transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCOUNT. SYNC is set to 'Y' The following table gives the txn codes that have to be defined in addition to any other txn codes. Field Name Interest liq acct Loan Deposit INT.CR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.DR.CAP Yes 392 382 No 391 381 INT.CORR.TXN Yes 396 386 No 395 385

        Parameters:
        param - the IntDrCap to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setLastDayIncl

        public void setLastDayIncl(TField value)
        Set the specified value for LastDayIncl
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field determines whether the cap date is considered for interest calculation or not. Valid inputs are 'Y' or NULL. 1. If 'Y', the interest calculation, will consider the balance as of the Cap date and post the entries with the value date of cap date + 1. 2. If null, in the interest calculation, the interest will be calculated for the balance of cap date -1, and the entries will be posted with the value date of processing date. In case of online loan repayment resulting in interest capitalisation/collection , LAST.DAY.INCL is considered to be 'N' even if LAST.DAY.INCL is 'Y' in AZ/APP Level. Validation This field is a noinput field for ANNUITY type of repayment.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field determines whether the cap date is considered for interest calculation or not. Valid inputs are 'Y' or NULL. 1. If 'Y', the interest calculation, will consider the balance as of the Cap date and post the entries with the value date of cap date + 1. 2. If null, in the interest calculation, the interest will be calculated for the balance of cap date -1, and the entries will be posted with the value date of processing date. In case of online loan repayment resulting in interest capitalisation/collection , LAST.DAY.INCL is considered to be 'N' even if LAST.DAY.INCL is 'Y' in AZ/APP Level.         public void setLoanIntAdjust(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for LoanIntAdjust
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used to decide whether interest adjustment is allowed or not in an ANNUITY or CREDIT-CARD type AZ loan account. Interest adjustment is a functionality by which interest payment could be lesser than the accrued interest amount and the remaining amount would be debited from suspense account of class AZINTADJ. The suspense account would be settled during the subsequent repayments. Interest adjustment is allowed only if this field is set to YES. Validation Rules : Holds YES or NO Input allowed only if ACCT.SYNC field is set to YES.

      • setLoanPreclose

        public void setLoanPreclose(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for LoanPreclose
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. Loan Preclose implies closing down of the loan a/c well before the ORIGINAL maturity date- where Credit will be to the Loan a/c and Debit will be to the Repay a/c. When entered the system automatically identifies the transaction code as an EVENT of Loan Preclose. The SYSTEM record must be defined in AZ.SETTLEMENT.PRIORITY file. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application. TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y".

        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setMaxInstlIntOnly

        public void setMaxInstlIntOnly(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for MaxInstlIntOnly
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Total period of time that the interest only repayment could be defined for a loan during the life time of a loan account. If input is given in numbers it is treated as number of days. If input is given prefixing P, it is treated as number of installments. Example: If input is given as 60, it implies that the total number of Interest Only repayment period cannot exceed 60 days during the life of the loan account. If input is given as P60, it implies that the total number Interest only repayment period cannot exceed 60 installments (of any frequency like daily, monthly) during the life of the loan account. Note: For loan accounts with repayment type 'Non Redemption', no validation will be done with respect to this field. Validation Rules Value for this field will be accepted only if 'INT ONLY' field is defined as Y Valid only for Loan Product Cannot have negative values

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Not allowed for CREDIT CARD type of products. Debit transaction code not allowed.

        Parameters:
        param - the OdChargeTxn to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setPayIntAtMat

        public void setPayIntAtMat(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PayIntAtMat
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used to decide whether accrued interest has to be paid out or rolled over during rollover of a fixed deposit. Allowed values are YES or NO If 'YES' is defined, then during rollover, the accrued interest before rollover will be paid out .When final maturity is reached or maturity instruction is Payment to Nominated account, then interest will be paid to Nominated account. If 'NO' is defined, then interest will be rolled over along with the principal deposit amount by default. The amount of rolled over deposit can anyway be overridden by the rollover amount definition at AZ.ACCOUNT level

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setPdLinkToAz

        public void setPdLinkToAz(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for PdLinkToAz
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field can be input as either 'YES' or 'NO' or ''. If this field is YES-an, attempt to repay an amount, less than the amount raised by way of schedules after repay date will create, PD. In this case APPLY.PENALTY must be set to 'N'.If PD is not installed, then the funds will be automatically debited from repay account. If this field is NO then, the amount still payable will continue to remain in the account (i.e., the principal will not be reduced) and AZ.OVERDUES will be updated. Allowed only if ACCT.SYNC is set to 'YES'. Not allowed for CREDIT CARD type of loan products. If this field is '' then, FT on hold will be created for the insufficient funds. VALIDATIONS YES or NO or ''. Value in this field should be same as that of ACCT.SYNC for loans Once input the values cannot be changed. Partial payment will raise PD only if repay date is past for credit cards.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setPenalOperand(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PenalOperand
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Determines the method by which the effective interest of the loan product (either a key based variable interest or fixed interest or a combination of both) is to be adjusted by the Penal margin to arrive at the penal interest rate. This field specifies whether the Margin Rate is to be added to, subtracted from or multiplied by the effective rate to arrive at the penal interest rate. If Multiply is specified the final rate is (100 + M) percent of the effective interest rate , where M is the Margin Rate percentage. Validation Rules Valid values are ADD, SUBTRACT or MULTIPLY. This field is available for input only when APPLY.PENALTY is y

      • setPenalRate

        public void setPenalRate(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for PenalRate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the penal rate of interest that can be applied on the value defined under the field PENALTY.ON. At present, the penalty interest rate is applied on the arrears amount only. When PENAL.OPERAND and PENAL.MARGIN are not defined, then this field is allowed for input by user. Otherwise, where the operand and margin values are defined, the penal rate will be calculated automatically by the system from the effective interest. If APPLY.PENALTY is set to 'Y' and PENAL.MARGIN, PENAL.OPERAND and PENAL.RATE are null the system would default the EFFECTIVE.INT.RATE into this field. The penal interest rate entered here is defaulted to AZ loan account. However, at account level it can be modified, in case of need. Validation Rules Rate type, numeric value Maximum value 100 Negative values not accepted.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setPenaltyCollAt

        public void setPenaltyCollAt(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PenaltyCollAt
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines when the charges defined in LATE.PYMT.FEE field in APP are to be collected when they are processed during COB. IMMEDIATE: The fee will be collected immediately while processing in COB. MATURITY: The fee will be carried forward till maturity of the deposit. This is applicable in the case of part withdrawal of deposit. NEXT-INSTALLMENT: In the case of part withdrawal of Savings Plan type, the fee will be adjusted in the next installment credited to the account. NEXT-INT-DUE: In the case of part withdrawal the fee will be adjusted in the next interest due for remaining deposit Validation Rules Valid values are, IMMEDIATE, MATURITY, NEXT-INSTALLMENT, NEXT-INT-DUe

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set

      • setPreCloseRtn

        public void setPreCloseRtn(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PreCloseRtn
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: A local routine with a valid PGM.FILE entry with PGM.TYPE set to 'S' can be attached in this field. This routine will be triggered when a part withdrawal or preclose of a deposit happens. If it is a multi deposit then this routine will be triggered for every sub account during preclosure / part withdrawal. This field is allowed only if PI.TABLE.TO.USE is set to OTHERS. The routine to be triggered will have to be input as 'LOCAL.ROUTINE(INTEREST.RATE)'. Where INTEREST.RATE is the rate that is returned from the routine. This rate will be used instead of EARLY.RED.MARGIN if any given.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setPreClosureFee(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)

        Field description: Defines the charges to be levied for pre-closure of the deposit / loan account or part withdrawal of deposit. These charges will be debited only if the pre-closure of the deposit / loan is done by using AZ.ACCOUNT. The withdrawals made through other channels like Teller or ATM, the system will not recognise the differential interest and the charges. In these cases, the pre-closure fee and differential fee are to be debited manually. Validation Rules Should be a valid charge code defined under FT.CHARGE.TYPE or FT.COMMISSION.TYPE.

      • setRateChngExist

        public void setRateChngExist(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RateChngExist
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field can take "Y", "N" or "null". When the field is input as "Y" or "" any change in rate of interest i.e. through Basic.Interest key will be effective not only to new accounts but the existing accounts will also be taken at the changed rate-from the date of such change. If "N" is input then any change in rate of interest will be applicable only to the new a/cs whose draw downs are after the date of such change.

        value - The value to set

      • setRateKey

        public void setRateKey(TField value)
        Set the specified value for RateKey
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Contains the linking reference number of the appropriate interest rate, which will be used for interest computation purposes. The key indicates the rate to be used for interest computation purposes on Loans and Deposit accounts. The key can take the form of an entry on the BASIC RATE TEXT and consequently BASIC INTEREST table. A rate change on the BASIC.INTEREST rate table will automatically reschedule the loan / deposit accounts that are linked to table, on the respective dates or on the dates defined as per the interest revision notice periods. This process will be done during COB. Validation Rules 1-2 numeric characters. (Optional input.) Should have been defined in BASIC.RATE.TEXT and in BASIC.INTEREST table

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRateOperand

        public void setRateOperand(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RateOperand
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Determines the method by which the basic interest rate is to be adjusted by the RATE.SPREAD to arrive at the Variable interest rate for this loan product. This field specifies whether the Spread Rate is to be added to, subtracted from or multiplied by the basic interest rate to arrive at the final variable interest rate. If Multiply is specified the final rate is (100 + M) percent of the effective interest rate , where M is the Margin Rate percentage. Validation Rules Valid values are ADD, SUBTRACT or MULTIPLY. This field is available for input only when RATE.KEY is defined

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRatePercent

        public void setRatePercent(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RatePercent
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the percentage of outstanding amount up to which the Variable interest rate is applicable. For the rest of the percentage amount, fixed interest rate will be applicable. Example: If 60 is defined here, variable interest will be applied on 60% of the outstanding amount and Fixed interest will be applied on the remaining 40% of the outstanding amount. The only EXCEPTION is FIXED-FLOATING type of deposit or loan-which takes only 100 as input in this field. Validation Rules 1-5 numeric rate type like 60, 45.50 etc. Maximum value 100. No negative values will be accepted. In case of FIXED-FLOATING type -this field has to be input with the value 100. In case this is defined then any change to the BASIC.INTEREST will not be applicable.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRatePeriod

        public void setRatePeriod(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RatePeriod
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Input in this field implies that the product is a Fixed Floating type. A Fixed Floating product initially takes a FIXED rate of interest and then moves to floating rate of interest till maturity based on the PERIOD input in the field RATE.PERIOD. Values may be input in the following format, i.e. nnD or nnM or nny The floating rate is prompted by 'R' schedule without which a FIXED FLOATING deposit or loan acct cannot be committed or authorized. The rates of interest both FIXED and FLOATING are defaulted from APP. A combination of the following interest is permitted for input, (1) BASIC.INTEREST (BI) and FIXED.RATE (2) BASIC.INTEREST (BI) and PERIODIC INTEREST (PI) To illustrate, In AZ.PRODUCT.PARAMETER the RATE.PERIOD is input as 03M. The Fixed Floating Deposit Start date is 05.04.2003 and maturity date is 04.04.2004. Interest is FIXED at 20% (field INT.FIXED.RATE) and for floating BI rate with RATE.KEY as 01 RATE.SPREAD as 2% RATE.OPERAND as ADD [Assume that the BI rate on the date of R schedule is 6.75%] System takes FIXED rate of interest at 20% from 05.04.2003 to 05.07.2003 And FLOATING rate at 8.75% (6.75% + 2%) from 06.07.2003 till 04.04.2004 Thus RATE.PERIOD is the field that differentiates a FIXED-FLOATING contract from other types of contracts. Based on the input in this field 'R' schedule is triggered to bring FLOATING rate in to operation. VALIDATIONS (1) Two numeric and One alphanumeric input allowed. (2) Permitted values in RATE.PERIOD nn>D, nn>M and nn>Y (3) Fixed and Floating interest rates are defaulted from APP- user has the option to change the FIXED rate of interest directly at account level and FLOATING rate by changing the INTEREST. RATE value in BI table. (4) The change in Rate. key value can be gauged from the ACI record only (5) Spread cannot be changed it is fixed. (6) For fixed floating a combination of BI + PI, BI + FIXED is allowed but not PI AND FIXED. (7) Not applicable for credit cards

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setReduceLimit

        public void setReduceLimit(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for ReduceLimit
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used to provide a revolving limit functionlity in loan products. If defined as '' then on the scheduled dates the limit is reduced for P and A schedules and incase of N schedules where there is no interest liquadation account, which provides a non-revolving functionlity. If defined as 'NO' then on the scheduled dates the limit is not reduced which provides a revolving limit functionlity. In this case the PRINCIPAL in AZ.ACCOUNT is not reduced on schedule dates or when the principal is repaid. Not allowed for deposits and CREDIT CARD. 'NO' not allowed for ANNUITY type of loans. If set to 'NO' then value in DRAWDOWN field cannot be set to 1, i.e., full drawdown. Allowed values are 'NO' or ''.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRepaymentType

        public void setRepaymentType(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RepaymentType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Repayment type of the All in One Accounts opened under this product. This type determines the way in which the loan / deposit account is to be repaid. The repayment types available for loan accounts are: 1. ANNUITY This type of loan has a fixed periodic repayment amount (the 'annuity') consisting of two variable components of principal and interest. The repayment amount is calculated at the start of the contract so that the principal will be fully repaid after the required number of repayments. Initially, repayments consist mostly of interest. However, as the contract progresses, the size of the principal component increases as the accrued interest reduces. In All in One loan account, for defining a zero repayment at the start of the loan, for a fixed period, Annuity type of repayment can be defined in the schedule with amount as Zero. 2. LINEAR Linear loans also have an interest and a principal component to their periodic repayments. In this case, however, the principal repayment amount remains fixed over the lifetime of the contract. The interest element reduces as the accrued interest on the reducing balance decreases. This leads to a repayment scheme whereby the total periodic repayment reduces over the lifetime of the contract. 3. NONRED In NONRED type of loans, there is no regular repayment of principal, but only interest. The redemption of Principal will be done on maturity date of the loan. In All in One account loans, the validations relating to Interest Only and Maximum Period interest only will not happen for this type of loan. 4. OTHER Non structured repayments are handled under this type. Repayment of any amount on any dates are allowed, provided the total repayment amount is equal to principal. 5.CREDIT CARD This type of Loan repayment type was added from G14.0.00. For this repayment type, the schedules are NO. When the repayment type is Credit Card the regular schedules are discarded, sub a/cs are created and new types of schedules like CI, CC are generated automatically. Repayment types available for Deposit accounts are: FIXED Deposit amount is accepted in a fixed lump sum and repaid as fixed amount either with interest accumulated or not. SAVING PLAN Deposit amount is accepted in a periodic basis and the principal is increased in a recurring manner till the end of a fixed term. Validation Rules 1 to 12 Alpha characters. Input must be either 'ANNUITY', 'LINEAR', 'OTHERS', 'NONRED' or 'CREDIT CARD' for loan products and 'SAVINGS PLAN' or 'FIXED' for Deposit products. Once defined and record authorised cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRevolvingRatio

        public void setRevolvingRatio(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RevolvingRatio
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Inputs in this field indicate that the product is a REVOLVING type. Input permitted is Numeric, which is applied to the total drawls made by the customer to arrive at the schedule repayment amounts by way of CC schedules. The ratio input in this field is defaulted to AZ main A/c. Input made can be altered at any time. VALIDATIONS Any numeric from 1-100 Allowed only for CREDIT CARD type of products.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRollMatWrkDay

        public void setRollMatWrkDay(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RollMatWrkDay
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field indicates if the rolled over new maturity date should be a working day or not. If the field is Yes, during rollover of loans & deposits, if the new maturity date happens to be on a holiday, then the system shall set the new maturity date to the first working day after the rolled over date. Assume that value date of AZ is 10th Aug 2005 & maturity date is 15th Aug 2005 . Then during rollover, the system shall set Value date as 15th Aug & new maturity date as 20th Aug. If the field is YES & 20th Aug happens to be a holiday & first working day after rollover is 22nd Aug , then new maturity date will be set to 22nd Aug. If the field is NO, then new maturity date will still be 20th Aug only. Allowed values - YES,NO. NO & null are treated the same.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRollMatWrkDay

        public void setRollMatWrkDay(TField value)
        Set the specified value for RollMatWrkDay
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field indicates if the rolled over new maturity date should be a working day or not. If the field is YES & 20th Aug happens to be a holiday & first working day after rollover is 22nd Aug , then new maturity date will be set to 22nd Aug. If the field is NO, then new maturity date will still be 20th Aug only. Allowed values - YES,NO. NO & null are treated the same.

      • setRolloverAcctng

        public void setRolloverAcctng(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RolloverAcctng
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field specifies if accounting entries over the AZ.ACCOUNT need to be raised during rollover. This could be useful for passbook printing purposes. For example, Let us assume that the deposit is for 5000. If the MATURITY.INSTR is 'AUTOMATIC ROLLOVER' then during rollover the following entries will be generated. A. Nominated account is given, Case 1. Rollover amount - 5000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Nominated a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Dr Nominated a/c 5000 Case 2. Rollover amount - 6000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Nominated a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 6000 Dr Nominated a/c 6000 Case 3. Rollover amount - 4000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Nominated a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 4000 Dr Nominated a/c 4000 B. No nominated account given, Case 1. Rollover amount - 5000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Internal a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Dr Internal a/c 5000 Case 2. Rollover amount - 6000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Internal a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 6000 Dr Internal a/c 6000 Create a TELLER.DEFAULT crediting AZ.ACCOUNT for 1000. Case 3. Rollover amount - 4000 Dr AZ.ACCOUNT 5000 Cr Internal a/c 5000 Cr AZ.ACCOUNT 4000 Dr Internal a/c 4000 Create a TELLER.DEFAULT debiting Internal account for 1000. MATURITY.DR txn code will be used on the debit side and ROLLOVER.CR txn code will be used on the credit side entries to AZ.ACCOUNT. If nominated account is not provided then an internal account will be used. The category of the internal account need to be defined in ACCOUNT.CLASS application for 'AZROLLOVER' id. Allowed only if ACCT.SYNC is set to 'Y'. Allowed only for FIXED type deposits.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setRolloverCr

        public void setRolloverCr(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for RolloverCr
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used when raising the credit entry during rollover of deposits. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y".

      • setSingleLimit

        public void setSingleLimit(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for SingleLimit
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field specifies the value that should be set in the SINGLE.LIMIT field in the ACCOUNT that is attached to this APP. Input can be 'Y', 'N' or ''. If input as 'Y' then the acct that is attached to the product parameter should also have the field single limit marked as yes. If input as 'N' or '' then the acct that is attached to the product parameter cannot have the field single limit marked as 'Y'. In this case all the AZ.ACCOUNT that are linked to the same limit must have REDUCE.LIMIT set to be the same. VALIDATIONS Input can be either 'Y', 'N' or ''.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setTaxOnIntTxn

        public void setTaxOnIntTxn(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)
        Set the specified TaxOnIntTxn to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Valid Transaction code should be entered. Txn codes that affect the loan/deposit side (Debit or Credit) are identified and categorized as TXN codes. This txn code is used to signify that the entry is a tax on interest entry when the TAX.KEY is defined in AZ.ACCOUNT. VALIDATIONS Must be a valid "ID" in transaction application TXN codes are input to identify the EVENT i.e. loan repay, Draw down etc. Mandatory input if the ACCT. SYNC is set to "Y". Both debit / credit transaction code allowed. Debit/Credit transaction code should be the same as the transaction code defined in TAX table. For instance, if TAX.KEY is defined as 10 in AZ.ACCOUNT, in the respective Tax table, the Credit/debit transaction code is defined as 243/244, then the same codes should be defined here.

        Parameters:
        param - the TaxOnIntTxn to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setTermPriority

        public void setTermPriority(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for TermPriority
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies whether the Term of the loan has to be prioritised and kept constant or not, in the case of Re scheduling. In AZ Loan accounts, the term of the loan or repayment amount may change due to certain factors like Principal increase, Principal decrease, change in Rate of interest, change in frequency etc. In such cases, it is possible to retain the original term and the maturity date as constant and change the repayment amount suitably, by specifying the Term Priority as 'Y'. If Term Priority is specified as 'N', then by keeping the repayment amount as constant the term will be changed by altering the maturity date of the loan. This field has to be opted by the user whenever a Rescheduling of the loan account is to be done. According to the value defined here, Rescheduling will be done and the previous schedule will be written to AZ.SCHEDULES.HIST. In case of annuity type of loans if the user defined annuity amount is greater than the system generated amount then the contract will be matured earlier than the actual maturity date even though this field is set to 'Y'. In case of OTHERS/NONRED type of loans, TERM.PRIORITY 'N' is not applicable as they may have uneven payments. Hence if AZ contract is of OTHERS/NONRED type of loans, then system shall ignore the value in this field and work as if TERM.PRIORITY is 'Y'. Validation Rules Valid value 'Y' or 'N'

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing
